### [51] [Performance Gap Analysis between Latin and Arabic Scripts HTR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18884)
*Sana Al-azzawi,Elisa Barney,Marcus Liwicki*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究通过统一的CRNN模型对九个阿拉伯语和拉丁语手写文本识别数据集进行线级识别，系统比较了两种脚本在不同训练规模下的表现。结果显示，阿拉伯语脚本在低资源情况下性能显著低于拉丁语，尽管随着数据量增加差距缩小，但在全量数据下仍存在5-7 CER点的差距。研究发现标注质量影响显著，清理错误可降低误差并缩小差距但无法消除。阿拉伯语因视觉变异性高，需更多数据才能学习到有效表示；同时，阿拉伯语字符频率分布更偏态，导致相同数量文本行或字符时覆盖能力较差。错误分析显示，约30%的阿拉伯语替换错误源于视觉相似字符混淆，而拉丁语仅为15%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解阿拉伯语手写文本识别（HTR）系统为何在性能上落后于拉丁语系统，尤其是在缺乏控制性比较的情况下，揭示根本原因以指导改进。

Method: 采用统一的CRNN模型，在九个跨语言、多语言的数据集（包括阿拉伯语、乌尔都语、波斯语、英语、德语等）上进行线级手写文本识别实验，涵盖不同训练规模（从100到完整数据集）。通过对比性能差异、标注质量影响、数据覆盖效率、字符频率分布及错误类型分析，系统评估影响因素。

Result: 阿拉伯语脚本在所有训练规模下均表现较差，尤其在低资源条件下差距明显；即使在全量数据下，仍保持5-7 CER点的性能差距。标注质量差是重要因素，清洗后误差下降且差距缩小，但未完全消除。阿拉伯语因视觉变异性高，需更多样本才能达到与拉丁语相当的表示能力。阿拉伯语字符频率分布更重尾，导致相同数量的文本行或字符在信息覆盖上不如拉丁语。错误分析显示，阿拉伯语中约30%的替换错误由视觉相似字符引起，远高于拉丁语的15%。

Conclusion: 阿拉伯语手写文本识别性能落后于拉丁语并非单一因素所致，而是由标注质量、视觉复杂性、字符分布特性以及数据需求差异共同作用的结果。提升阿拉伯语HTR性能需综合优化数据质量、扩大训练规模，并针对性设计模型以处理视觉相似字符的混淆问题。

Abstract: Recent studies have shown that handwritten text recognition (HTR) systems perform worse on Arabic-script datasets than on Latin-script data. However, the reasons for this gap are still not well understood due to the lack of controlled comparisons. In this work, we present a comprehensive study of Arabic and Latin scripts HTR using a unified CRNN model for line-level HTR across nine datasets (including KHATT (Arabic), Muharaf (Arabic), NUST-UHWR (Urdu), PHTD (Persian), IAM (English), READ-2016 (German), and others) and di ferent training sizes (K in {100, 500, 1000, 2000, ..., Kfull}). Our results show the performance gap remains: it is large in low-resource settings, decreases with more data, but remains even at full scale, with a consistent difference of 5-7 CER points. We show that annotation quality matters, as many datasets contain labeling errors. Cleaning reduces error rates and narrows the gap, but does not eliminate it. In addition, we find that a fixed number of training samples provides less effective coverage in Arabic due to higher visual variability, requiring more data to learn similar representations. We compare recognition across datasets in terms of the number of text lines and the number of characters, showing an equivalence trade-off. We compare character frequency distributions across scripts and show that Arabic is significantly more heavy-tailed than Latin. Our error analysis reveals that around 30 percent of substitution errors in Arabic datasets (e.g., KHATT) are caused by confusion between visually similar characters, compared to about 15 percent in Latin-script datasets such as IAM.

Method: 提出LARE（Low-Attention Region Encoding）框架，采用双编码策略，同时编码图像的低关注度区域和完整图像，生成更具多样性和信息量的嵌入表示。

Abstract: Image retrieval in crowded scenes is particularly challenging due to the salience bias of conventional visual encoders, which tend to focus on dominant objects while neglecting low-attention regions that are often crucial for fine-grained retrieval. We propose LARE (Low-Attention Region Encoding), a framework that explicitly models these overlooked regions. LARE adopts a dual-encoding strategy that encodes low-attention regions of an image and the full image in parallel, leading to more diverse and informative image embeddings. To evaluate image retrieval performance in challenging crowded scenes, we introduce Dense-Set, a challenging subset derived from COCO and Flickr30K. In this subset, images are re-captioned to provide richer descriptions of low-attention or previously overlooked regions. This dataset highlights the limitations of existing retrieval models and enables a more rigorous evaluation under densely crowded scene conditions.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Although DINOv3 has demonstrated remarkable semantic discrimination in natural imagery, its direct application to volumetric medical segmentation is hindered by inherent dimension and domain disparities. Subsequently, we further enhance volumetric understanding by adding lightweight 3D adapters into the frozen backbone to enforce global inter-slice continuity. Finally, to compensate for the spatial information loss inherent in the embedding process, we design a parallel detail recovery stream to explicitly preserve high-frequency boundary cues. Extensive experiments on five public datasets demonstrate that our approach successfully adapts DINOv3 to the medical domain and significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines.

### [54] [Automatic ply-specific analyses of CFRP micrographs using shortest-path-based ply distinction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18894)
*Jonas Naumann,Jonas P. Appels,Julius Biermann,Christopher Gorsky,Timo de Wolff,Christoph Brauer*

TL;DR: 提出一种自动化方法，通过将语义分割掩码视为图结构并使用最短路径算法识别铺层边界，实现高分辨率碳纤维复合材料显微图像中铺层实例的分割。该方法利用全局信息桥接语义分割与铺层实例分割之间的差距，并成功应用于具有多种复杂特征（如人工间隙、不同堆叠顺序和铺层裂纹）的图像。基于计算出的路径可对每个纤维像素进行铺层分配，进而实现对局部纤维体积分数、铺层及夹层厚度等微观结构特性的定量分析，揭示制造引起的非均质性，为优化制造参数和建立力学性能与微观缺陷之间的联系提供支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语义分割方法无法区分同一类别中的不同实例（如铺层），导致难以进行精细化的微观结构分析。为解决这一问题，需要一种能够利用全局信息区分铺层实例的方法，以实现对复合材料微观结构的精确量化分析。

Method: 将语义分割掩码视为图结构，其中像素作为顶点；通过最短路径算法识别铺层间的分隔路径；基于这些路径将每个纤维像素分配至对应的铺层。

Result: 成功在包含多种复杂特征的高分辨率图像上实现铺层实例分割；获得局部纤维体积分数、铺层及夹层厚度等关键微观结构参数；揭示制造过程中的非均质性，支持制造参数优化与性能关联分析。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效结合语义分割与全局路径信息，实现了高精度铺层实例分割，为复合材料微观结构的定量分析提供了新工具，有助于理解制造缺陷与材料性能之间的关系。

Abstract: We present an automated approach to distinguish between ply instances in semantic segmentation masks of high-resolution carbon-fiber reinforced polymer micrographs. Interpreting the segmentation mask as a graph with pixels as vertices, enables us to use a shortest-path algorithm yielding the ply-separating paths. Thereby, we bridge the gap between semantic segmentation and ply instance segmentation using global information. We successfully apply our approach on high-resolution micrographs featuring a broad range of characteristics like artificially added gaps in single or multiple plies, different stacking sequences and ply traversing cracks. Assigning each fiber pixel to a ply based on the calculated paths, allows for a comprehensive, quantitative ply analysis with respect to its microstructural properties like the local fiber volume fraction as well as locally resolved ply and interleaf layer thickness. These insights help to reveal manufacturing-induced inhomogeneities, draw conclusions on manufacturing parameters and link mechanical properties to underlying microstructural imperfections.

</details>


### [55] [BindEdit: Taming Attention Leakage for Precise Multi-Object Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18906)
*Chaewon Park,Soyoon Lee,Naeun Lee,Minjung Shin,Seogkyu Jeon,Kibeom Hong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: BindEdit提出一种在单次扩散轨迹中施加注意力约束的方法，以解决真实图像编辑中的语义混叠、对象重复和编辑不完整问题。通过抑制编辑令牌泄漏（Edit-Token Leakage）和源主导泄漏（Source Dominance Leakage），结合交叉注意力重平衡与区域保真度项，实现精准的多对象编辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在复杂多对象场景下易出现语义混叠、对象重复或编辑不完整，根源在于去噪过程中空间区域与文本标记之间的注意力泄漏，尤其表现为编辑令牌对齐模糊和未改变源对象的语义主导。

Method: BindEdit通过联合正则化交叉注意力与自注意力，使目标标记组与其对应空间区域绑定并保持实例分离；引入交叉注意力重平衡机制增强目标标记影响、抑制源语义残留；同时加入区域保真度项确保目标概念在编辑掩码内一致表达。

Result: 在包含多种对象数量与类别的综合性多对象基准测试中，BindEdit显著优于现有方法，在单对象与多对象编辑场景下均表现出鲁棒且一致的性能提升。

Conclusion: BindEdit有效缓解了注意力泄漏问题，实现了更精确、可靠的多对象图像编辑，为真实世界图像编辑提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Real image editing enables precise manipulation of visual content, yet existing methods often fail in complex multi-object scenarios, causing semantic blending, object duplication, or incomplete edits. We attribute these failures to attention leakage, where signals across spatial regions and text tokens become entangled during the denoising process. Specifically, we identify two distinct forms of leakage: Edit-Token Leakage, where ambiguous token-region alignment leads to object blending, and Source Dominance Leakage, where tokens of unchanged source objects overwhelm the attention intended for target entities. To resolve these leakages, we propose \textbf{BindEdit}, which enforces attention-level constraints within a single diffusion trajectory. To suppress Edit-Token Leakage, BindEdit jointly regularizes cross- and self-attention so that each target token group is bound to its corresponding spatial region while maintaining instance-level separation. To suppress Source Dominance Leakage, a cross-attention re-balancing mechanism amplifies target token influence and attenuates residual source semantics within editable regions. Moreover, a region fidelity term ensures that each target concept is expressed coherently across the entire editing mask. Additionally, we propose a comprehensive multi-object benchmark encompassing diverse object counts and categories. Extensive experiments demonstrate that BindEdit consistently outperforms existing methods within a single diffusion trajectory, maintaining robust performance across both single- and multi-object editing scenarios.

</details>


### [56] [Physics-IQ Verified](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18943)
*Tim Rädsch,Yuki M Asano,Hilde Kuehne,Stefan Bauer,Priyank Jaini,Robert Geirhos,Carsten T. Lüth*

Method: 通过系统性审计Physics-IQ基准，识别出提示与真实样本中的混淆因素；提出优化策略，包括提升提示与真实样本质量，设计样本级评分机制，使每个样本和评价指标具有同等权重；最终构建Physics-IQ Verified基准，并进行多模型对比验证。

Result: Physics-IQ Verified成功优化了57.6%的样本，改进了34.8%的提示；在六种图像到视频生成模型的比较中，排名变化显著（Kendall's $τ= 0.46$），表明该基准能更准确反映模型的物理理解能力。

Conclusion: Physics-IQ Verified通过提升评估标准的严谨性与公平性，为衡量VGMs的物理理解能力提供了更可靠、更可比的基准，有望推动该领域向更真实、更可信的方向发展。

Abstract: Video generative models ( VGMs) have become a new frontier that can be used not just for video generation but for a multitude of downstream tasks, including world modeling. To advance these tasks, a good video model must understand the physical reality of the world. Evaluating this understanding is an emerging field and has led to the Physics-IQ benchmark, which quantifies this explicitly by comparing model-generated videos to real-world videos of physical experiments. In this work, we present a systematic audit of the Physics-IQ benchmark, expose shortcomings and propose three solutions that sharpen how we can measure physical understanding of VGMs. Specifically, we improve prompt and ground-truth quality to reduce the influence of confounding factors and further introduce a sample-level scoring system that weights each sample and metric equally. Our resulting benchmark, Physics-IQ Verified, refines 57.6\% of all samples and improves over 34.8\% of prompts. In a comparison study using six image-to-video generative models, we observe moderate but meaningful ranking changes (Kendall's $τ= 0.46$). We hope Physics-IQ Verified advances the community by providing a more reliable signal toward physically accurate VGMs. The code for the benchmark can be accessed at https://github.com/google-deepmind/physics-iq-benchmark

### [59] [Mem-World: Memory-Augmented Action-Conditioned World Models for Persistent Robot Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18960)
*Zirui Zheng,Jiaqian Yu,Xiongfeng Peng,jun shi,Mingyi Li,Chao Zhang,Weiming Li,Dong Wang,Huchuan Lu,Xu Jia*

Method: 提出Mem-World，核心为W-VMem——一种4D腕部视图中心的surfel索引记忆结构，将历史观测锚定于随时间演化的表面元素上，支持基于未来动作的几何感知历史帧检索；通过surfel渲染与评分机制选择生成过程中的关键历史帧，以提供高效、非冗余的上下文信息。

Result: Mem-World在复杂操作任务中实现了持久化视频回放；在政策评估中比Ctrl-World提升14.5%的皮尔逊相关性；通过合成数据生成显著提升策略性能，长时任务成功率由58%增至72%。

Abstract: Action-conditioned world models have emerged as a promising paradigm for robot learning, offering a scalable alternative to costly real-world experimentation by generating action-consistent video rollouts. However, persistent world modeling remains challenging in manipulation: frequent end-effector occlusions and rapid wrist-camera motion make the current observation insufficient for predicting future views, causing models to forget or hallucinate scene details seen in earlier frames. Existing memory retrieval strategies often fail to identify informative history in dynamic manipulation scenarios. To address this limitation, we propose Mem-World, a memory-augmented multi-view action-conditioned world model. At its core, we present W-VMem, a 4D wrist-view-centered surfel-indexed memory that anchors historical observations to temporally evolving surface elements. By explicitly modeling when and where scene elements are observed, W-VMem enables geometry-aware retrieval of relevant history frames conditioned on future actions. During generation, relevant history frames are selected via surfel-based rendering and scoring, providing informative and non-redundant context for prediction. Extensive experiments show that Mem-World generates persistent rollouts in complex manipulation scenarios, enables more reliable policy evaluation than Ctrl-World, improving the Pearson correlation with real-world performance by 14.5\%, and supports effective policy improvement through synthetic data generation, increasing success rates from 58\% to 72\% on long-horizon tasks.

### [60] [Visual-OPSD: Cross-Modal On-Policy Self-Distillation for Efficient Unified Multimodal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18974)
*Pengyu Li,Zhitao Gao,Lingling Zhang,Muye Huang,Yuanming Li,Fangzhi Xu,Jun Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Visual-OPSD方法，通过教师-学生框架在无需生成视觉思考的情况下将推理知识迁移到文本模型中，在多个基准上显著提升性能并大幅加速推理，证明了生成路径中的语义信息对性能的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 统一多模态模型中的视觉思考（VTs）虽能提升空间任务表现，但其带来的推理成本高昂且实际收益有限；研究发现即使移除或噪声化VTs，准确率变化不大，说明注意力集中在渲染后的图像而非内容本身，但条件信息仍影响模型输出分布，提示生成过程蕴含额外推理价值。

Method: 提出视觉就地自蒸馏（Visual-OPSD），教师与学生共享权重，但教师可访问特权视觉思考轨迹，学生仅接收问题；通过在学生采样轨迹上进行令牌级JSD蒸馏，将教师的推理能力迁移到纯文本学生模型中。

Conclusion: 生成过程中的视觉思考不仅提供像素结果，其内在语义路径也承载重要推理信息；通过就地自蒸馏可高效提取该信息，实现高性能、低延迟的多模态推理。

Abstract: Unified multimodal models (UMMs) interleave generated ''visual thoughts'' (VTs) with text reasoning to improve spatial tasks. This incurs roughly an order-of-magnitude inference cost from multi-step diffusion. We find this cost yields limited direct benefit. On ThinkMorph, removing or noising VTs barely changes accuracy across nine benchmarks. Once rendered, attention concentrates on the VT regardless of content. Yet a KL diagnostic shows that conditioning on a privileged VT trace shifts the model's completion distribution. This suggests the generation pathway encodes useful reasoning beyond the rendered pixels. Motivated by this gap, we propose Visual On-Policy Self-Distillation(Visual-OPSD). Teacher and student share identical weights but differ in context: the teacher sees privileged VTs while the student sees only the question. Token-level JSD distillation on on-policy student trajectories transfers the teacher's reasoning to a text-only student. Across nine benchmarks, Visual-OPSD improves over its generative teacher by $+3.40$pp with $14.3\times$ speedup (10.0s vs. 142.8s per sample) and outperforms same-scale VLMs by $+63.83$pp on VSP. A Gaussian-noise control ($+0.40$pp vs. $+10.28$pp for real VTs) and $58.4\%$ closure of the KL gap confirm that gains come from the semantic content of the generation pathway.

</details>


### [61] [Show, Don't Ask: Generative Visual Disambiguation for Composed Image Retrieval with Turn-Valid Coverage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18992)
*Amsisan Tran,Baogh Le,Tuan Kiet Pham,Sui Yang Guang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CLARA is a visual clarification framework for composed image retrieval that addresses ambiguity by showing users a panel of visual alternatives instead of relying on text questions. It maintains conformal prediction coverage across multiple interactions by reweighting calibration via likelihood ratios based on user selections, and ensures prototype images are grounded in the real corpus to prevent artificial coverage inflation. Experiments show CLARA matches state-of-the-art single-turn performance, preserves nominal coverage over rounds, and achieves faster convergence—especially in cases involving viewpoint or fine-grained attributes.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing methods for composed image retrieval struggle with ambiguous queries that describe multiple possible images. While conformal prediction and text-based clarifying questions help, they suffer from limited coverage after the first interaction and often fail to resolve subtle visual differences due to the limitations of textual description.

Method: CLARA introduces a visual clarification mechanism where users select the most similar image from a small panel of prototypes. The system dynamically updates the candidate set, reweights calibration using likelihood ratios derived from user choices, and constrains prototypes to real images from the corpus to ensure valid coverage guarantees across multiple interaction rounds.

Result: CLARA achieves retrieval performance comparable to state-of-the-art single-turn methods, maintains nominal coverage across multiple interaction rounds, and finds the correct target image in fewer rounds than text-question baselines. It particularly excels in resolving ambiguities related to viewpoint and fine-grained visual attributes, where visual feedback outperforms text-based questioning.

Conclusion: By replacing text-based clarifications with visual prototype selection and leveraging likelihood ratio-based recalibration, CLARA effectively resolves ambiguity in composed image retrieval while preserving statistical validity across interactions. This approach is especially powerful for fine-grained visual distinctions, demonstrating the superiority of direct visual feedback in complex retrieval tasks.

Abstract: Composed image retrieval (CIR) uses a reference image and a text modification to search for a target image. However, such queries often describe several possible images rather than one exact target, making the user's intent ambiguous. Recent methods address this by using conformal prediction to estimate ambiguity and by asking users clarifying text questions. However, these methods have two limitations: their coverage guarantee only holds at the first interaction, and text questions are often insufficient for resolving fine-grained visual differences such as appearance, attributes, or viewpoint. We propose CLARA, a clarification framework that resolves ambiguity by showing users a small panel of visual alternatives. Instead of answering text questions, the user simply selects the prototype image closest to the intended target. This provides a direct visual signal and avoids relying on a model to predict the user's answer. To maintain valid conformal guarantees across multiple interaction rounds, CLARA reweights calibration using the likelihood ratio induced by the user's selection. The displayed prototypes are also constrained to represent the current candidate set and are snapped to real corpus images, ensuring that generated images cannot artificially improve coverage. Experiments on open-domain and fashion benchmarks show that CLARA matches single-turn state-of-the-art retrieval performance, maintains nominal coverage across interaction rounds, and finds the intended target in fewer rounds than strong text-question baselines. Its advantage is especially clear when ambiguity involves viewpoint or fine-grained attributes, where visual clarification is more effective than textual questioning.

</details>


### [62] [FlowObject: Flow Steering for Bridging Generative Priors and Reconstruction Fidelity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19019)
*Yuchen Rao,Xuqian Ren,Yinyu Nie,Sayan Deb Sarkar,Biao Zhang,Vincent Lepetit,Friedrich Fraundorfer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FlowObject提出一种无需训练的双空间引导逆问题框架，通过流匹配模型的ODE轨迹引导，结合3DGS优化阶段，实现稀疏视角下3D重建中未观测区域的完整几何补全与真实观测一致性，显著提升几何完整性与视图依赖外观保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型存在合成偏差，过度依赖先验而忽略实际观测；优化方法如3DGS虽在可见表面高保真但无法推断不可见几何。两者难以同时保证几何完整性和观测一致性，尤其在严重遮挡下表现不佳。

Method: 提出FlowObject框架，采用双空间引导策略，指导流匹配模型的常微分方程（ODE）轨迹，在生成过程中融合学习到的先验以补全未观测区域，同时严格对齐真实观测数据；后续引入3DGS精修阶段，提升结果的逼真度。

Result: 在合成与真实数据集上的全面评估表明，该方法在几何完整性与视图依赖外观保真度方面均显著优于当前最先进生成模型和基于优化的方法，尤其在严重遮挡场景下优势明显。

Conclusion: FlowObject成功实现了生成与优化的优势融合，为稀疏视角3D重建提供了高效、高保真的解决方案，具备良好的泛化能力与实用性。

Abstract: Recovering complete 3D representations of objects from few casual image captures remains a significant challenge. Recent 3D generative models, particularly those based on Flow-Matching (FM), can synthesize high-quality textured assets; however, they often suffer from ''synthetic bias'' where learned priors override observational evidence, alongside a lack of alignment with the observed instance. Conversely, optimization-based methods like 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) provide high fidelity on visible surfaces but fail to reason about unobserved geometry. In this paper, we present FlowObject, a framework that reformulates sparse-view 3D reconstruction as a training-free, guided inverse problem. Our approach applies a dual-space guidance strategy to steer the Ordinary Differential Equation (ODE) trajectory of a flow-matching model, enabling the completion of unseen regions through learned generative priors while enforcing strict consistency with real-world observations. By integrating a 3DGS refinement stage, FlowObject further bridges the gap between ''synthetic-looking'' generative outputs and photorealistic reconstructions. Comprehensive benchmarks on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that current state-of-the-art methods often struggle to achieve geometric completeness and observational consistency simultaneously, especially under severe occlusions. In contrast, our method significantly outperforms state-of-the-art generative models and optimization-based frameworks in both geometric completeness and view-dependent appearance fidelity.

### [63] [Low-Rank Tensor Completion Based on Fractional Regularization with Ky Fan p-k Norm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19046)
*Shan Fan,Feng Zhang,Jianjun Wang,Xi-Le Zhao,Tingwen Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的非凸代理函数TNPK（张量核范数与张量Ky Fan p-k范数之比），用于更准确地逼近张量管秩，具有尺度不变性、参数灵活性及特定参数下的闭式解。该方法在低秩张量补全（LRTC）中表现出色，理论证明低秩张量是局部极小值，并设计了基于ADMM的高效算法，具备子序列收敛性。实验表明其优于现有先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低秩张量补全方法在逼近张量管秩时存在精度不足或计算复杂的问题，亟需更精确且高效的非凸代理函数来提升补全性能。

Method: 提出新型非凸代理函数TNPK，构建基于该范数的低秩张量补全模型；利用张量零空间性质证明低秩张量为局部最优解；推导Ky Fan p-k逆范数的近端算子，开发ADMM算法实现高效求解。

Result: 在合成数据和真实数据集上均取得优于当前最先进方法的补全效果，验证了所提方法的有效性和优越性。

Conclusion: 所提出的TNPK代理函数及其对应的优化框架在低秩张量补全任务中表现优异，兼具理论保障与实际性能优势，为张量补全提供了新思路。

Abstract: This paper addresses low-rank tensor completion (LRTC) by proposing a novel nonconvex surrogate, namely the ratio of the tensor nuclear norm to the tensor Ky Fan p-k norm (TNPK), to accurately approximate the tensor tubal rank. The TNPK possesses appealing properties, including scale invariance, parameter flexibility, and the existence of closed-form solutions under specific choices of p and k. With specific parameter settings of p and k, it reduces to the ratio of the tensor nuclear norm to the tensor Ky Fan k norm (TNK) or the ratio of the tensor nuclear norm to the tensor Frobenius norm (TNF). We construct a LRTC model and, under the tensor null space property (NSP), prove that low-rank tensors are local minimizers of the proposed model. Moreover, we derive the proximal operator of the Ky Fan p-k inverse-norm and further develop an efficient alternating direction method of multipliers (ADMM) algorithm with guaranteed subsequential convergence under mild conditions. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world datasets validate the superior performance of our method against state-of-the-art competitors.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）的评估多集中于整体或特定任务，缺乏对其在细粒度图像任务中能力的深入理解，而细粒度识别是计算机视觉的基础能力之一，亟需系统化评估工具。

Method: 提出FG-BMK基准，涵盖1.01百万问题和0.28百万图像，覆盖广泛场景；采用人导向与机器导向双范式，评估对话级细粒度语义识别与特征级视觉可区分性，支持对模型失败原因的诊断分析。

Conclusion: FG-BMK为细粒度视觉任务提供了全面评估框架，揭示了当前LVLMs的核心局限，并为未来更可靠模型的设计与数据构建提供重要指导。

Abstract: Recent advancements in Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) have demonstrated remarkable multimodal perception and reasoning capabilities. To address this gap, we introduce FG-BMK, a comprehensive fine-grained evaluation benchmark containing 1.01 million questions and 0.28 million images, covering diverse scenarios from common object-centric domains to specialized domains. FG-BMK jointly evaluates dialogue-level fine-grained semantic recognition and feature-level visual discriminability through human-oriented and machine-oriented paradigms, enabling diagnostic analysis of whether LVLM failures arise from insufficient visual representations, weak visual-to-semantic grounding, or limited fine-grained knowledge. We further analyze training design factors for improving fine-grained capabilities and examine how visual and linguistic perturbations affect LVLM predictions. Our code is open-source and available at https://fg-bmk.github.io/.

DREAM incorporates a hybrid language modeling strategy that combines masked and permuted language modeling objectives to capture both local and global linguistic semantics. Thus, we first introduce HOI-Edit, a comprehensive benchmark with three progressive cognitive levels, which features an automated metric HOI-Eval that reliably evaluates instance-level interaction by letting VLM Q&A after thinking with images containing grounded Human-Object pairs. Considering the task's essence of remodeling dynamic relationships, we benchmark Image-to-Video (I2V) models, finding them inherently suited for dynamic editing due to their temporal generation capabilities. Crucially, beyond superior performance, this capability provides a "replay of the failure process," offering unique diagnosability into why errors occur. We thus propose SCPE (Self-Correcting Process Editing), a novel, agentic self-correcting framework that constrains the generation of I2V models through iteratively refined prompts, enabling the generated videos to more accurately present the target HOI. Extracted frames from these videos are the final editing results. On HOI-Edit, SCPE achieves performance competitive with state-of-the-art (SOTA) editing models like Nano Banana on interaction. ### [68] [DVANet: Degradation-aware Visual-prior Alignment Network for Image Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19097)
*Yanjie Tu,Qingsen Yan,Axi Niu,Tao Hu,Haokui Zhang,Jiantao Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出DVANet，一种基于半二次分裂优化算法的深度展开网络，用于统一图像恢复任务。该方法通过退化感知观测一致性与视觉先验引导重建的协同展开过程，实现对复杂退化下多样退化的适应性恢复。其中，退化表示模块提取全局退化属性和局部退化线索，并通过退化条件映射增强模型对不同退化类型的适应能力；视觉先验分支引入DINOv3提供分层结构与语义信息，以补充受损区域缺失的结构信息，提升细节恢复效果。实验表明，DVANet在多场景退化与跨域恢复任务中表现优异，具备良好的退化适应性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端图像恢复方法将恢复过程视为黑箱映射，缺乏可解释性；而现有深度展开方法多依赖固定退化假设或预定义退化信息，难以适应复杂退化和局部损伤，限制了其在退化抑制与结构细节恢复方面的性能。因此，亟需一种兼具可解释性、自适应性与强泛化能力的统一恢复框架。

Method: 提出DVANet，基于半二次分裂优化算法构建深度展开网络，设计双分支协同机制：1）退化感知观测一致性分支，利用退化表示模块提取全局与局部退化特征，并通过退化条件映射提升适应性；2）视觉先验引导重建分支，引入DINOv3作为层次化视觉先验，提供结构与语义信息以增强受损区域的细节恢复。

Result: 在多种复杂退化场景和跨域图像恢复任务上，DVANet均取得优于或相当现有方法的性能，验证了其在退化适应性、结构恢复与泛化能力方面的优势。

Conclusion: DVANet通过融合退化感知与视觉先验的协同展开机制，在保持优化可解释性的同时，显著提升了统一图像恢复框架对复杂退化和局部损伤的处理能力，为未来通用图像恢复提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: All-in-One image restoration aims to develop a unified restoration framework for handling diverse degradation types. Existing end-to-end methods usually regard the restoration process as a black-box mapping, lacking an explicit optimization interpretation. Although deep unfolding provides an interpretable iterative modeling paradigm for image restoration, existing methods mostly rely on fixed degradation assumptions or predefined degradation information, making them difficult to adapt to unified restoration requirements under complex degradations and locally damaged content. This limitation restricts their performance in degradation suppression and structural detail recovery. To address these issues, this paper proposes DVANet, a deep unfolding network inspired by the half-quadratic splitting optimization algorithm, which formulates unified image restoration under complex degradations as a collaborative unfolding process between degradation-aware observation consistency and visual-prior-guided reconstruction. Specifically, in the degradation-aware observation consistency branch, a degradation representation module is employed to extract global degradation attributes and local degradation cues, and degradation-conditioned mapping is used to enhance the model's adaptability to different degradation types. In the visual-prior-guided reconstruction branch, DINOv3 is introduced to provide structural and semantic information as hierarchical visual priors, thereby complementing the missing structural information in damaged regions and improving detail recovery. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DVANet achieves superior or competitive performance on multi-scenario degradation and cross-domain image restoration tasks, showing favorable degradation adaptability and generalization ability.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源多模态大模型普遍将欧洲葡萄牙语（pt-PT）与巴西葡萄牙语混淆或严重忽视，导致pt-PT在多模态任务中缺乏有效支持，亟需一个专为pt-PT设计的高质量开放模型。

Result: AMALIA-VL在多项评估中展现出对欧洲葡萄牙语多模态任务的强大性能，建立了首个面向pt-PT的开源多模态大模型基准。所有模型权重、训练数据和开发工具将公开，促进该语言的多模态研究生态发展。

Conclusion: AMALIA-VL成功填补了欧洲葡萄牙语在开源多模态大模型中的空白，为未来多语言、多模态系统的公平性与包容性提供了重要范例。

Abstract: Large Vision and Language Models (LVLMs) have advanced rapidly, yet European Portuguese (pt-PT) remains systematically underserved by existing open-source multimodal models, which either conflate it with Brazilian Portuguese or severely under-represent it in their training data mixes. We introduce AMALIA-VL, the first open-source instruction-tuned LVLM built natively for pt-PT, pairing a high-resolution vision encoder with dynamic image tiling and a fully open pt-PT-optimized language model via a learned connector. We contribute with a purposefully designed three-stage training process - vision-language alignment, general visual instruction tuning, and preference optimization - together with a pt-PT-centric multimodal data mix combining curated and translated public datasets with novel datasets that address the near-total absence of European Portuguese multimodal resources. Our evaluation shows that AMALIA-VL establishes a strong baseline for open-source pt-PT LVLMs.We will release model weights, training data, and construction pipelines along with machine-translated pt-PT evaluation benchmarks to help democratize pt-PT LVLM development.

### [70] [ProductConsistency: Improving Product Identity Preservation in Instruction-Based Image Editing via SFT and RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19103)

Abstract: Recent advances in instruction-based image editing have enabled models to perform complex visual edits from natural language instructions.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Hand-4DGS框架，采用网格引导的表示学习结构先验，并结合时空卷积建模手部动态；利用高斯点阵实现有效的2D图像监督，无需3D手部姿态真值标注。

Abstract: Dynamic 3D hand reconstruction from egocentric videos is essential for next-generation computing platforms such as AR/VR and AI glasses. Despite its importance, most prior works focus either on multi-view 3D hand reconstruction or on 4D human body reconstruction. Egocentric 4D hand reconstruction remains challenging due to fast head motion, rapid hand dynamics, severe occlusions, and inherent ambiguity from single-view observations. To address these challenges, we introduce Hand-4DGS, the first feed-forward framework for reconstructing dynamic 4D hands directly from egocentric videos, enabling both fast (~60 FPS) inference and strong generalization. Our approach incorporates a mesh-guided representation for structural priors and temporal convolutions to model dynamic motion. We evaluate our framework on two challenging egocentric datasets, H2O and ARCTIC, and demonstrate significant improvements over baselines. Our method benefits from the generalization capability of feed-forward networks and effective 2D image supervision through Gaussian splatting, without requiring expensive 3D hand pose ground-truth annotations.

### [73] [When AUC Misleads: Polarization-Aware Evaluation of Deepfake Detectors under Domain Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19184)
*Dat Nguyen,Cosmin Radoi,Romain Hermary,Marcella Astrid,Nesryne Mejri,Enjie Ghorbel,Djamila Aouada*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的深度伪造检测评估指标——跨数据集AUC（Cross-AUC），通过结合各领域AUC与预测极化度（用Wasserstein距离衡量）来更真实地反映检测器在混合数据源和不同伪造类型下的泛化能力。该方法提升了评估的现实意义和可解释性，实验验证了其在七个基准数据集上的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度伪造检测评估方法仅在单一数据集上计算AUC，无法反映真实世界中多源数据混合、伪造类型多样等复杂场景，导致评估结果与实际性能脱节。

Method: 提出Cross-AUC指标，综合考虑各数据集的AUC值，并引入Wasserstein距离量化类别得分分布的极化程度，以评估模型对域偏移的鲁棒性。

Result: 在七个基准数据集上的实验表明，Cross-AUC能更准确、可解释地评估深度伪造检测器的真实泛化能力，有效揭示性能下降的原因。

Conclusion: Cross-AUC是一种更贴近现实、更具解释性的深度伪造检测评估方法，有助于推动检测技术向更可靠的实际应用发展。

Abstract: Recent advances in generative AI, such as diffusion models and face-swapping tools, have enabled the creation of highly realistic deepfakes, leading to real-world harms including financial fraud and non-consensual explicit content. In response, deepfake detection has become an active research area, with recent methods increasingly focusing on improving generalization to unseen manipulations. This is typically evaluated using the Area Under the ROC Curve (AUC) measured separately across multiple datasets. However, such an evaluation fails to reflect real-world scenarios where detectors face a mixture of data sources and varying artifact types. To address this limitation, we introduce a novel metric, Cross-dataset AUC (Cross-AUC) that averages per-domain AUCs with a measure of prediction polarization for taking into account the robustness to domain shift. The polarization extent is quantified by the Wasserstein Distance between class score distributions. Cross-AUC not only assesses the generalization capabilities of deepfake detectors under domain shifts more realistically, but it is also interpretable as it better explains the reason behind a drop in performance. Experiments performed on seven benchmark datasets demonstrate its practical relevance.

</details>


### [74] [Moebius: 0.2B Lightweight Image Inpainting Framework with 10B-Level Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19195)
*Kangsheng Duan,Ziyang Xu,Wenyu Liu,Xiaohu Ruan,Xiaoxin Chen,Xinggang Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Moebius 是一个高效轻量级图像修复框架，通过引入局部-λ混合交互（LλMI）模块重构扩散模型主干，将空间上下文和全局语义先验压缩为固定大小的线性矩阵，显著减少参数量的同时保持复杂潜在交互。结合自适应多粒度蒸馏策略，在潜空间内动态平衡多种梯度损失，实现高保真生成。实验表明，Moebius 仅用不到2%的参数（0.22B vs. 11.9B），推理速度提升15倍以上，性能媲美甚至超越100亿级工业通用模型FLUX.1-Fill-Dev，树立了高质量图像修复的新效率标杆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有100亿级工业基础模型虽在图像修复上表现优异，但计算成本过高，难以实际部署。而任务专用轻量模型因结构极度压缩导致表征瓶颈，限制了性能发挥。因此亟需一种既能极大降低参数量与计算开销，又能保持高生成质量的轻量级修复框架。

Method: 提出Moebius框架，核心包括：(1) 设计LλMI块，包含局部-λ与交互-λ模块，将空间上下文和全局语义信息压缩为固定尺寸线性矩阵，实现高效特征表示；(2) 提出自适应多粒度蒸馏策略，基于潜空间中的多种梯度损失动态调整，优化生成质量而不依赖像素空间解码。

Result: 在自然图像与人像修复基准上，Moebius 在仅使用0.22B参数（不足11.9B的2%）的情况下，推理速度超过15倍于基线，生成质量可媲美甚至优于100亿级通用模型FLUX.1-Fill-Dev，验证了其卓越的效率与性能平衡。

Conclusion: Moebius成功实现了高保真图像修复在极低参数量与超快推理速度下的突破，证明了通过结构创新与训练策略协同优化，轻量级专用模型可在关键任务中超越大型通用模型，为高效生成模型设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: While 10B-level industrial foundation models have pushed the boundaries of image inpainting, their prohibitive computational costs severely hinder practical deployment. Constructing a highly optimized task-specific specialist offers a promising solution; however, extreme structural compression inevitably triggers a severe representation bottleneck. To conquer this, we propose Moebius, a highly efficient lightweight inpainting framework. We systematically reconstruct the diffusion backbone by introducing the Local-$λ$ Mix Interaction ($LλMI$) block. Comprising Local-$λ$ and Interactive-$λ$ modules, it elegantly summarizes spatial contexts and global semantic priors into fixed-size linear matrices, preserving complex latent interactions while drastically shedding parameters. Furthermore, to unlock the full representational capacity of this highly compact architecture, we synergistically pair it with an adaptive multi-granularity distillation strategy. Operating strictly within the latent space to avoid expensive pixel-space decoding, this strategy dynamically balances multiple gradient-based losses to achieve high-fidelity alignment. Extensive experiments across natural and portrait benchmarks demonstrate that this optimal synergy enables Moebius to rival or even surpass the generation quality of the 10B-level industrial generalist FLUX.1-Fill-Dev. Remarkably, Moebius achieves this using less than 2\% of the parameters (0.22B vs. 11.9B) while delivering a $>15\times$ acceleration in total inference time, setting a new efficiency standard for high-fidelity inpainting. Project page at https://hustvl.github.io/Moebius.

</details>

*Kaustubh Kapil,Kishor P. Upla*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了Transformer Geometry Observatory (TGO)框架，用于系统研究视觉变压器（ViT）的表示几何与动态特性。TGO-I聚焦于ViT表示的谱几何，通过分析训练过程中有效秩、稳定秩、参与度比率、谱熵、谱平坦度、谱各向异性、协方差结构、特征值谱和奇异值谱等指标，发现随着训练进行，维度利用率持续上升，各向异性下降，谱熵和参与度比率增加，特征值谱趋于平坦。这一现象表明信息并未集中到少数主导方向，而是逐渐在更多维度间重新分布，尤其在最终的CLS token表示中表现最为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管视觉变压器（ViTs）在计算机视觉任务中广泛应用且表现优异，但其维度与表示几何的基本理解仍不充分。为填补这一空白，本文旨在深入探究ViT的表示几何特性，揭示其训练过程中的动态变化规律。

Method: 提出并应用Transformer Geometry Observatory (TGO)框架，具体使用ViT-Small/16模型在ImageNet-100上进行训练，并系统分析多个表示几何指标，包括有效秩、稳定秩、参与度比率、谱熵、谱平坦度、谱各向异性、协方差结构、特征值谱和奇异值谱等，以追踪训练过程中的变化。

Result: 实验结果显示，随着训练进行，维数利用度持续增加，各向异性下降，谱熵和参与度比率上升，特征值谱趋于平坦。特别是最终的CLS token表示展现出最高的有效维度和最低的各向异性，表明信息在训练过程中被广泛分布在更多维度上，而非集中在少数主导方向。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了视觉变压器在训练过程中表示空间的演化规律：信息并非集中于少数主成分，而是逐步扩散至更广泛的维度空间。这挑战了传统直觉，并为理解ViT的表征机制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Despite the widespread adoption of Vision Transformers (ViTs) and their success across numerous computer vision applications, the fundamental understanding of their dimensional and representational geometry remains relatively underexplored. To address this gap, we introduce Transformer Geometry Observatory (TGO), a systematic framework of experiments and analysis pipelines designed to investigate the representational geometry and dynamics of Vision Transformers. TGO-I, the first installment of the framework, focuses on the spectral geometry of ViT representations. Using a ViT-Small/16 model trained on ImageNet-100, we analyze Effective Rank, Stable Rank, Participation Ratio, Spectral Entropy, Spectral Flatness, Spectral Anisotropy, covariance structure, eigenspectra, and singular value spectra throughout training. Our results reveal a consistent increase in dimensional utilization, accompanied by decreasing anisotropy, increasing spectral entropy, increasing participation ratio, and progressively flatter eigenspectra. Contrary to the common intuition that training should concentrate information into a small number of dominant directions, we observe a progressive redistribution of variance across representational dimensions. This phenomenon is particularly pronounced in the final CLS token representation, which exhibits the highest effective dimensionality and lowest anisotropy within the network.

</details>


### [78] [OneCanvas: 3D Scene Understanding via Panoramic Reprojection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19253)
*Bartłomiej Baranowski,Dave Zhenyu Chen,Matthias Nießner*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OneCanvas提出一种无需复杂几何编码器或大量训练预算的3D场景理解方法，通过将多视角图像块投影到等距圆柱全景画布上，保留3D空间位置信息，并引入3D位置嵌入恢复深度信息。该方法使视觉语言模型能以统一空间坐标系处理多视角数据，支持从特定视角进行情境化推理，适用于机器人和具身AI。此外，通过程序化生成带标签的3D空间监督信号，构建空间预训练课程，有效减少空间推理捷径。实验表明，OneCanvas在SQA3D、VSI-Bench上达到顶尖性能，并在SPBench上展现良好泛化能力，训练计算量仅为强基线方法的十分之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖复杂的几何编码器或高计算成本来实现3D空间推理，难以高效支持具身智能中的情境化理解任务。需要一种轻量、通用且能支持灵活视角推理的3D表示方法。

Method: 将多视角图像块根据其深度与相机位姿反投影至3D世界坐标，映射到一个等距圆柱全景画布上的连续经纬度位置，不进行重采样或融合；为每个图像块添加基于其真实3D坐标的嵌入，以恢复因投影丢失的深度信息；利用预训练视觉语言模型直接处理该画布表示，实现端到端推理；设计程序化空间预训练课程，通过在空画布上放置来自真实图像的对象块并控制答案分布，生成多样化的空间推理监督信号。

Result: OneCanvas在SQA3D和VSI-Bench上达到当前最优性能，在SPBench上表现出优异的分布外泛化能力，且训练所需计算资源仅为最强对比方法的约1/10，显著提升效率与实用性。

Conclusion: OneCanvas提供了一种高效、通用且可扩展的3D场景理解框架，无需修改骨干网络即可实现跨视角空间推理，支持情境化任务与轻量化训练，为具身智能系统中的视觉-语言协同提供了新范式。

Abstract: Existing approaches to 3D scene understanding in Vision-Language Models (VLMs) either rely on complex, model-specific geometry encoders or large training budgets in pursuit of spatial reasoning. Instead, OneCanvas aggregates patch features from all views onto a single equirectangular panoramic canvas. Namely, each patch is unprojected to a 3D world coordinate using its depth and camera pose, then placed on the canvas at the continuous longitude and latitude of that point as seen from the canvas origin, with no rasterization or aggregation across overlapping views. A 3D position embedding of the patch's metric coordinates is added to its feature, restoring the depth lost when collapsing the world position to an angular canvas coordinate. Patches from all frames thus share one spatial coordinate system with no fusion or major architectural modifications of the backbone. The pretrained VLM consumes this representation as if it were an ordinary image. Because the canvas can be centered on any pose of interest, the same representation directly supports situated reasoning from a specific viewpoint, a common requirement in robotics and embodied AI. Thanks to this representation, we can also introduce a spatial pretraining curriculum: by procedurally placing patch features of objects, drawn from real images, at chosen 3D world positions on an otherwise empty canvas, we generate on-the-fly supervision spanning a broad range of spatial reasoning tasks, with answer distributions controlled to reduce spatial reasoning shortcuts. OneCanvas achieves state-of-the-art accuracy on SQA3D and VSI-Bench, and generalizes to out-of-distribution data on SPBench, using an order of magnitude less training compute than the strongest competing methods.

</details>


### [79] [Native Active Perception as Reasoning for Omni-Modal Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19341)
*Zhenghao Xing,Ruiyang Xu,Yuxuan Wang,Jinzheng He,Ziyang Ma,Qize Yang,Yunfei Chu,Jin Xu,Junyang Lin,Chi-Wing Fu,Pheng-Ann Heng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OmniAgent 是首个原生多模态代理，将视频理解建模为基于 POMDP 的迭代观察-思考-行动循环，通过按需执行动作选择性提取音视频线索并存入持久文本记忆，有效解耦推理复杂度与原始视频时长。提出两种关键技术：(1) 代理监督微调（ASFT）实现主动感知的初始化；(2) 基于 TAURA（Turn-aware Adaptive Uncertainty Rescaled Advantage）的代理强化学习，利用回合级熵引导信用分配至关键发现回合。该模型具备测试时正向扩展性，性能随推理回合数增加而提升，在十个基准测试中表现领先，7B 版本在 LVBench 上超越 10 倍更大的 Qwen2.5-VL-72B 模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统被动模型对长视频采用均匀处理，计算成本随视频长度线性增长；现有交互式框架依赖全局预扫描，上下文开销仍与视频长度相关。亟需一种能动态、高效理解长视频的主动感知机制。

Method: 提出 OmniAgent，基于 POMDP 构建迭代观察-思考-行动框架，通过按需动作选择性提取多模态信息并写入持久文本记忆；引入 Agentic Supervised Fine-Tuning 实现初始主动感知能力；设计 Agentic Reinforcement Learning with TAURA，利用回合级不确定性调整优势信号，精准激励关键探索行为。

Result: OmniAgent 在十项基准测试（如 VideoMME、LVBench）上达到开源模型最优性能；其 7B 版本在 LVBench 上以 50.5% 准确率超越 72B 的 Qwen2.5-VL-72B（47.3%），且性能随推理回合数上升，验证主动感知有效性。

Conclusion: OmniAgent 成功实现了长视频理解中推理复杂度与视频长度的解耦，通过主动感知和智能决策显著降低计算开销，同时提升性能，为大规模视频理解提供了高效、可扩展的新范式。

Abstract: Passive models for long video understanding typically rely on a "watch-it-all" paradigm, processing frames uniformly regardless of query difficulty, causing computational cost to grow with video duration. Although interactive frameworks have emerged, they often rely on global pre-scanning, and their context cost still scales with video length. We propose OmniAgent, the first native omni-modal agent that formulates video understanding as a POMDP-based iterative Observation-Thought-Action cycle. OmniAgent executes on-demand actions to selectively distill audio-visual cues into a persistent textual memory, effectively decoupling reasoning complexity from raw video duration. To operationalize this, we introduce (1) Agentic Supervised Fine-Tuning to bootstrap native active perception via best-of-N trajectory synthesis with dual-stage quality control, and (2) Agentic Reinforcement Learning with TAURA (Turn-aware Adaptive Uncertainty Rescaled Advantage), which leverages turn-level entropy to steer credit assignment toward pivotal discovery turns. Crucially, OmniAgent exhibits positive test-time scaling, where performance improves as the number of reasoning turns increases, validating the efficacy of active perception. Empirical results across ten benchmarks (e.g., VideoMME, LVBench) demonstrate that OmniAgent achieves state-of-the-art performance among open-source models. Notably, on LVBench, our 7B agent outperforms the 10$\times$ larger Qwen2.5-VL-72B (50.5% vs. 47.3%).

</details>


### [80] [CABLE: Cloud-Assisted Bandwidth-efficient LMM-based Encoding for V2X Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19258)
*Haohua Que,Zhipeng Bao,Qianyi Wu,Handong Yao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CABLE 是一种云辅助的高效带宽多模态模型（LMM）编码框架，通过在边缘-云之间传递分割掩码并利用运动补偿与残差运动线索，仅上传感兴趣区域（ROI）图像，显著降低通信开销和云端预填充延迟。实验表明，在多个数据集上实现了73%-87%的像素覆盖率减少和5-8倍的LMM预填充加速，同时保持较好的感知性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有云托管的大规模多模态模型虽能提供强大的开放词汇感知能力，但直接传输全分辨率帧会导致严重的通信开销和高云端预填充延迟，亟需一种高效的边缘-云感知框架以降低资源消耗。

Method: CABLE 采用基于运动补偿的前一帧云分割掩码传播机制，结合残差运动线索进行细化，并通过走廊包络合并断开区域，形成鲁棒的感兴趣区域（ROI）。仅将ROI掩码覆盖的图像上传至云端，同时将云端输出作为下一帧的先验，构建了从掩码到ROI再到LMM的反馈循环。

Result: 在nuScenes、WOD-ZB、Waymo、KITTI和CADC五个数据集上的实验表明，CABLE实现了73%-87%的ROI像素覆盖率减少，以及5-8倍的估计LMM预填充速度提升，检测质量略有下降但整体感知性能保持良好。

Conclusion: CABLE通过设计高效的边缘-云协同感知架构，显著降低了通信成本和计算延迟，为车辆-万物系统中的大规模多模态感知提供了可行且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Cloud-hosted large multimodal models (LMMs) can provide strong open-vocabulary perception for Vehicle-to-Everything systems, but naively transmitting full-resolution frames from edge to cloud causes severe communication overhead and high cloud-side prefill latency. We present CABLE, a cloud-assisted bandwidth-efficient LMM-based encoding framework for edge-cloud perception. CABLE propagates the previous cloud segmentation mask on the edge using ego-motion compensation, refines it with residual-motion cues, and consolidates disconnected regions via a corridor envelope to form a robust region of interest (ROI). Only ROI-masked images are uploaded, while the cloud segmentation output is fed back as the prior for the next frame, forming a mask-to-ROI-to-LMM feedback loop. Experiments on five datasets (nuScenes, WOD-ZB, Waymo, KITTI, and CADC) show consistent communication savings while largely preserving perception, achieving $73$--$87\%$ ROI pixel-coverage reduction with $5$--$8\times$ estimated LMM prefill speedup at a modest detection-quality trade-off relative to full-frame inference.

</details>

Existing benchmarks, however, largely focus on object-centric images and provide limited coverage of scenarios where textual semantics and layout organization are central. In this paper, we introduce a multi-domain benchmark for detecting text-rich images generated by OpenAI's GPT Image 2. The benchmark contains 8,602 images across six representative categories: commercial posters, infographics, academic posters, receipts, tables, and UI screenshots. Using this benchmark, we evaluate five representative AI-generated image detectors in a zero-shot setting and analyze their overall, category-wise, and post-processing robustness. These findings highlight the need for text- and layout-aware detection methods for modern AI-generated images. Our dataset is released at XXX.

Abstract: Visual Question Answering (VQA) in the Remote Sensing (RS) domain presents unique challenges due to the high resolution, multi scale object distribution, and semantic complexity of aerial imagery. While general domain Foundation Models have achieved remarkable success, their direct application to RSVQA is hindered by massive domain shifts and the computationally prohibitive nature of full fine tuning. This study presents a comparative analysis of RS Adapter, a Parameter Efficient Fine Tuning (PEFT) strategy, applied across three distinct Vision Language Model (VLM) architectures: the Dual Encoder CLIP, the Encoder Decoder BLIP, and the Hybrid FLAVA. We introduce a unified architectural surgery pipeline that injects lightweight bottleneck adapters into the attention and MLP layers of frozen backbones, enabling rapid adaptation with less than 5 percent of trainable parameters. Experimental results on the high resolution RSVQA x dataset demonstrate that while all adapted models achieve convergence, the Hybrid FLAVA architecture offers a superior balance of multimodal reasoning and retrieval capabilities compared to its unimodal counterparts. Our findings establish a new baseline for resource efficient VQA in disaster assessment and urban monitoring.

### [83] [Confidence is Not Reliability: Rethinking MC Dropout in Brain Tumour Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19300)
*Xin Ci Wong,Duygu Sarikaya,Kieran Zucker,Marc De Kamps,Nishant Ravikumar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了在多参数MRI中使用蒙特卡洛丢弃（MC Dropout）进行体素级不确定性估计，以识别胶质瘤分割中临床关键区域的错误。实验基于126名BraTS21患者，比较了预训练的SegResNet和本地训练的UNet-Res模型。结果显示，MC Dropout在保持分割精度的同时，实现了强不确定性与错误的对齐（熵的AUROC≈0.97），表明不确定性能有效区分错误与正确体素。基于熵的患者分层发现高不确定性组分割性能显著下降（全肿瘤Dice中位数0.835 vs. 0.925），支持不确定性作为实际分诊信号。然而，全局对齐可能掩盖区域特异性差异：尽管两模型AUROC相似，但UNet-Res在增强肿瘤区域表现出极低熵（0.054）和高预期校准误差（ECE=0.915），Dice仅0.714，表明其在最临床关键区域严重误校准，这一问题无法通过标准的Dice或AUROC指标暴露。因此，强不确定性-错误对齐虽必要，但不足以保障临床安全；模型部署前必须结合区域特异性校准评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于重叠的评估指标（如Dice分数）无法揭示模型在治疗关键区域的隐性失败，而临床安全要求模型在这些区域具备可靠且可校准的不确定性估计。因此，亟需评估不确定性估计是否能有效识别关键区域错误，并判断校准失败是否可通过常规报告指标发现。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛丢弃（MC Dropout）进行体素级不确定性估计，在126名BraTS21患者上对比预训练SegResNet与本地训练的UNet-Res模型。通过计算熵（H）的AUROC评估不确定性与分割错误的对齐程度，利用熵对患者分层，并分析不同子区域（如增强肿瘤）的不确定性分布与校准情况（如预期校准误差，ECE）。

Result: MC Dropout在保持分割精度（|ΔDice|<0.01）的前提下，实现了高不确定性-错误对齐（熵的AUROC≈0.97）。基于熵的患者分层显示高不确定性组整体分割性能显著下降（中位数Dice 0.835 vs. 0.925）。然而，尽管全局AUROC表现良好，UNet-Res在增强肿瘤区域呈现极低熵（0.054）和高ECE（0.915），Dice仅为0.714，表明其在关键区域存在严重校准偏差，该问题未被标准指标捕捉。

Conclusion: 强不确定性-错误对齐是必要的，但不足以确保临床安全；在选择用于临床部署的模型时，必须结合区域特异性校准评估，不能仅依赖全局指标如Dice或AUROC。

Abstract: Glioma segmentation in multiparametric MRI is a critical component of treatment planning. A segmentation model that fails silently on treatment-critical sub-regions represents a patient safety risk that overlap-based metrics such as Dice scores cannot expose. We ask whether voxel-level uncertainty estimation via Monte Carlo (MC) Dropout can reliably identify segmentation errors in clinically critical sub-regions, and whether calibration failure modes are detectable from standard reporting metrics alone. In an empirical two-model case study on 126 BraTS21 patients, we evaluate a high-performance pretrained SegResNet and a locally trained UNet with residual units (UNet-Res). MC dropout preserved segmentation accuracy ($|Δ\text{Dice}|$ $<0.01$) while achieving strong uncertainty-error alignment (AUROC for entropy (H) $\approx$0.97), indicating uncertainty correctly ranks erroneous voxels above correct ones. Entropy-based patient stratification identified a high-uncertainty subgroup with substantially lower segmentation performance (median whole-tumour Dice $0.835$ vs. $0.925$), supporting uncertainty as a practical triage signal. However, global alignment can mask important region-specific differences. Despite similar AUROC, UNet-Res exhibited near-zero enhancing tumour entropy ($0.054$) and Expected Calibration Error (ECE) of $0.915$, with a Dice of only $0.714$, indicating severely miscalibrated confidence on the most clinically critical sub-region, a failure mode invisible to standard Dice and AUROC reporting. These findings demonstrate that strong uncertainty-error alignment is necessary but insufficient for clinical safety: sub-region-specific calibration assessment must accompany AUROC evaluation when selecting models for clinical deployment.

</details>


### [84] [NeuMesh++: Towards Versatile and Efficient Volumetric Editing with Disentangled Neural Mesh-based Implicit Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19316)
*Chong Bao,Yuan Li,Bangbang Yang,Yujun Shen,Hujun Bao,Zhaopeng Cui,Yinda Zhang,Guofeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于网格的新型表示方法，通过在网格顶点上编码解耦的几何、纹理和语义代码，实现高效且全面的编辑功能，包括网格引导的几何编辑、指定纹理编辑（如纹理替换、填充和绘画）以及语义引导的编辑。为实现这些功能，作者设计了局部空间参数化以提升渲染质量与训练稳定性，引入可学习的顶点修改颜色以提高纹理编辑保真度，采用空间感知优化策略实现精确纹理编辑，并利用语义辅助区域选择减少隐式场编辑中繁琐的标注工作。大量实验和编辑示例表明，该方法在表示质量和编辑能力方面均表现出优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经渲染方法在编辑功能上受限，仅支持刚性变换和特定类别编辑，缺乏灵活性与通用性。为解决这一问题，需要一种能够支持多样化、精细控制的编辑操作的新表示方法。

Method: 提出一种基于网格的神经辐射场表示，将几何、纹理和语义信息解耦并编码于网格顶点；设计局部空间参数化以增强渲染质量与训练稳定性；引入可学习的顶点修改颜色以提升纹理编辑保真度；采用空间感知优化策略实现精准纹理编辑；使用语义辅助区域选择降低人工标注负担。

Result: 在真实和合成数据集上的大量实验表明，该方法在渲染质量、编辑灵活性和操作精度方面均优于现有方法，支持多种复杂编辑任务，且具有良好的可视化效果和实用性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的NeuMesh++通过解耦的网格表示和一系列创新技术，实现了高效、灵活且高质量的三维场景编辑，为神经隐式渲染的交互式编辑提供了新范式。

Abstract: Recently neural implicit rendering techniques have evolved rapidly and demonstrated significant advantages in novel view synthesis and 3D scene reconstruction. However, existing neural rendering methods for editing purposes offer limited functionalities, e.g., rigid transformation and category-specific editing. In this paper, we present a novel mesh-based representation by encoding the neural radiance field with disentangled geometry, texture, and semantic codes on mesh vertices, which empowers a set of efficient and comprehensive editing functionalities, including mesh-guided geometry editing, designated texture editing with texture swapping, filling and painting operations, and semantic-guided editing. To this end, we develop several techniques including a novel local space parameterization to enhance rendering quality and training stability, a learnable modification color on vertex to improve the fidelity of texture editing, a spatial-aware optimization strategy to realize precise texture editing, and a semantic-aided region selection to ease the laborious annotation of implicit field editing. Extensive experiments and editing examples on both real and synthetic datasets demonstrate the superiority of our method on representation quality and editing ability. Project page: https://zju3dv.github.io/neumeshplusplus/

### [85] [Beyond the Current Observation: Evaluating Multimodal Large Language Models in Controllable Non-Markov Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19338)
*Shengyuan Ding,Xilin Wei,Xinyu Fang,Haodong Duan,Dahua Lin,Jiaqi Wang,Yuhang Zang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RNG-Bench 是一个用于评估多模态基础模型在闭环策略中重建并利用不可见历史观测能力的基准测试套件，包含 Matching Pairs 和 3D Maze 两个游戏，通过控制网格大小、视觉模式和观测模态三个难度维度进行评估。引入对弈协议与 Memory Gap 指标以分离遗忘与决策误差，结果显示当前前沿多模态大模型在高复杂度任务上仍有显著提升空间，且通过最优策略微调可有效提升性能并迁移至其他基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法有效分离模型对隐藏状态的重建能力与其他技能，或仅在回合结束后测试记忆，难以真实反映多步交互中持续记忆与决策的能力。本文旨在建立一个能独立评估模型在非马尔可夫环境中重建过去观测并据此行动的基础能力的基准。

Method: 提出 RNG-Bench 基准，包含 Matching Pairs 和 3D Maze 两种游戏；设计统一测试框架，控制网格大小、视觉模式和观察模态三类难度变量；引入头对头对决机制以减少实例偏差；定义 Memory Gap 指标以区分遗忘与动作选择失误。

Result: 最困难配置需处理约 128K tokens 与 350 张图像输入，远未达到当前前沿多模态大模型的性能饱和；Memory Gap 分析表明，大部分残余错误源于早期观测的遗忘而非决策不佳；对 Qwen3.5-9B 进行基于最优策略回放与过滤演示的微调后，性能显著提升，并在不损害通用多模态能力的前提下迁移到其他基准。

Conclusion: RNG-Bench 能有效隔离并评估模型在非马尔可夫环境中的长期记忆与推理能力，揭示了当前多模态大模型在复杂记忆任务上的瓶颈主要来自遗忘而非决策问题；通过针对性微调可显著提升模型表现并实现跨任务泛化。

Abstract: Deploying multimodal foundation models as closed-loop policies increasingly requires conditioning actions on observations that are no longer visible. However, existing benchmarks either expose the full state, conflate hidden-state reconstruction with other agent skills, or test recall only after an episode has ended. We introduce RNG-Bench (Reconstructive Non-Markov Games), a benchmark suite designed to isolate a base model's ability to reconstruct past observations and act on them during multi-step interaction. RNG-Bench includes two complementary games: Matching Pairs, where card identities briefly revealed at specific locations must later be recalled, and 3D Maze, where egocentric views must be integrated into a spatial map. Both games are evaluated under a unified harness with three controlled difficulty axes: grid size, visual pattern, and observation modality. The benchmark further introduces a head-to-head duel protocol to control for instance-level variance and a Memory Gap metric that disentangles forgetting from poor action selection. The hardest configurations require contexts of roughly 128K tokens and 350 image inputs per episode, and remain far from saturated by frontier MLLMs. Memory Gap analysis shows that most residual errors stem from forgetting earlier observations rather than from suboptimal decision making. Finally, fine-tuning Qwen3.5-9B on optimal-policy rollouts and filtered model demonstrations improves performance on RNG-Bench and transfers to existing benchmarks without degrading general multimodal capability.

</details>

### [86] [Continuous Audio Thinking for Large Audio Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18273)
*Gyojin Han,Dong-Jae Lee,Changho Choi,Jongsuk Kim,Junmo Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出CoAT框架，通过连续潜在工作空间在生成响应前组织声学信息，利用专家蒸馏提供丰富的声学细节，提升音频语言模型在语音理解、音乐分类、情感识别等任务上的表现，且无需额外自回归解码开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大音频语言模型（LALMs）在训练中侧重文本对齐输出，导致其隐藏状态逐渐偏向文本生成，丢失了语音中的丰富声学信息（如发音细节、语调、声音事件、情感、音高等），难以有效利用这些信息进行高质量响应。

Method: 引入连续声学思维（CoAT）框架，构建一个连续的潜在工作空间，通过从音频专家中蒸馏知识来组织和保留声学信息；该思维块可在一次预填充中处理，避免增加自回归解码成本。

Result: 在Qwen2-Audio、Qwen2.5-Omni-7B和Audio Flamingo~3三个模型上，CoAT在涵盖音频推理、理解、音乐分类、语音情感和语音转录的广泛基准测试中均取得显著性能提升；分析表明辅助监督信号可从思维位置传递至最终文本输出。

Conclusion: CoAT成功增强了大音频语言模型对声学信息的保留与利用能力，提升了多类音频任务的表现，同时保持高效推理，为音频理解模型的设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large audio language models (LALMs) have shown impressive capabilities on diverse audio understanding tasks, ranging from speech transcription to music analysis. However, because LALMs are typically trained to produce text-aligned responses, their hidden states are progressively shaped for text generation rather than for preserving acoustic information. As a result, the diverse acoustic content that audio carries, such as phonetic detail, prosody, sound events, affect, and pitch, is lost along the way and difficult to leverage in the response. We introduce Continuous Audio Thinking (CoAT), a framework that equips audio language models with a continuous latent workspace for organizing acoustic information prior to response generation, grounded by distillation from audio experts. Within the thinking space, the model can utilize the rich acoustic information provided by expert distillation when generating its response. Furthermore, the proposed continuous thinking block can be processed in a single prefill, so CoAT does not require additional autoregressive decoding cost over the baseline. Across three LALMs, Qwen2-Audio, Qwen2.5-Omni-7B, and Audio Flamingo~3, performance gains on a broad benchmark suite spanning audio reasoning, audio understanding, music classification, speech emotion, and speech transcription demonstrate the effectiveness of CoAT. Further analysis confirms that the auxiliary supervision propagates from the thinking positions to the model's textual responses.

</details>


### [87] [Redact or Keep? A Fully Local AI Cascade for Educational Dialogue De-Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18372)
*Haocheng Zhang,Zhuqian Zhou,Kirk Vanacore,Bakhtawar Ahtisham,René F. Kizilcec*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种完全本地的级联框架，将教育对话中的去标识化从开放实体识别重构为受控隐私筛选。通过双轻量编码器与确定性规则联合生成候选片段，再由上下文感知的审查器基于对话上下文和说话人角色判断是否删除。在数学辅导对话数据上，最优本地配置达到0.958宏F1，显著优于同族LLM基线（0.767）和商用API（0.706），且可在单台笔记本运行。在课程术语与真实姓名混淆的挑战集上，性能仅下降0.03 F1，远优于其他小模型。结果表明，在教育去标识化中，问题建模比模型规模更为关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 教育对话包含真实学习过程，但也混杂个人身份信息（PII）与课程内容，如'黎曼'可能指学生或数学概念。现有方法在治理与准确性之间存在权衡：商用大模型虽能处理歧义但需外传数据，本地命名实体识别系统则过度删减课程术语。因此亟需一种既能保护隐私又不损害教学内容完整性的本地化解决方案。

Method: 提出全本地级联框架，包括：(1) 召回优先的联合提议器，结合两个轻量编码器与确定性规则生成候选实体；(2) 上下文感知审查器，根据对话上下文和说话人角色对每个候选做二分类（删除/保留）。整个流程无需外部依赖，可部署于本地设备。

Result: 在两个大型平台的数学辅导对话数据上，最强本地配置获得0.958宏F1，优于同家族LLM基线（0.767）和商用API（0.706），且仅需单台笔记本运行。在针对课程-个人名称歧义的挑战集上，该配置性能仅下降0.03 F1，而较小审查器下降达0.19–0.25。

Conclusion: 对于教育去标识化任务，问题的重新定义（即从实体识别转为隐私三策）比单纯依赖大模型规模更有效。本地化、基于规则与上下文感知的设计可实现高准确率与强数据治理的兼顾。

Abstract: Educational dialogue is a valuable but sensitive resource for research: the same transcripts that capture authentic learning often capture personally identifiable information (PII) entangled with curricular content, where "Riemann" may refer to a real student or to a mathematical concept. Existing approaches force a tradeoff between governance and accuracy. Commercial Large Language Models (LLMs) can handle this ambiguity but require sending student data to third parties, while local named entity recognition (NER) systems preserve governance but over-redact curricular terms. We propose a fully local cascade framework that reframes de-identification from open-ended entity recognition to constrained privacy triage. A recall-first union proposer combines two lightweight encoders with deterministic rules to over-generate candidate spans; a context-aware reviewer then makes a binary Redact/Keep decision for each candidate using surrounding dialogue and speaker role. We evaluate three reviewer configurations against same-family LLM-only baselines and a commercial API on math tutoring transcripts from two large platforms. The strongest local configuration reaches 0.958 macro F1, compared with 0.767 for a same-family LLM-only baseline and 0.706 for the commercial API, while running entirely on a single laptop. On a targeted challenge set of curricular-personal name ambiguity, the same configuration degrades by only 0.03 F1 versus 0.19 to 0.25 for smaller reviewers. These results suggest that for educational de-identification, problem formulation matters more than model scale.

</details>


### [88] [SproutRAG: Attention-Guided Tree Search with Progressive Embeddings for Long-Document RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18381)
*Amirhossein Abaskohi,Issam H. Laradji,Peter West,Giuseppe Carenini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SproutRAG 是一种基于注意力引导的层次化 RAG 框架，通过学习句子间注意力来构建二叉分块树，实现多粒度检索，无需额外大模型调用或摘要压缩，在多个基准上平均提升信息效率 6.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 RAG 方法在检索粒度与上下文连贯性之间难以平衡，依赖大模型分块、单一粒度扩展或有损摘要，导致成本高或信息丢失。

Method: 利用学习到的跨句注意力构建层次化分块树，通过端到端训练优化嵌入与树结构，检索时采用层次化束搜索实现多粒度候选生成。

Result: 在科学、法律和开放域四个基准上，相比最强基线，信息效率平均提升 6.1%。

Conclusion: SproutRAG 有效解决了检索粒度与上下文连贯性的权衡问题，实现了无需额外大模型调用的多粒度检索，且在多个领域表现优越。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems must balance retrieval granularity with contextual coherence, a challenge that existing methods address through LLM-guided chunking, single-level context expansion, or hierarchical summarization. These approaches variously depend on costly LLM calls during indexing or retrieval, limit context aggregation to a single granularity level, or introduce information loss through summarization. We present SproutRAG, an attention-guided hierarchical RAG framework that addresses this trade-off by organizing sentence-level chunks into progressively larger but semantically coherent units, using learned inter-sentence attention to construct a binary chunking tree. Unlike prior approaches that rely on external LLMs, fixed context expansion, or lossy summarization, SproutRAG learns which attention heads and layers best capture semantic document structure, enabling multi-granularity retrieval without additional LLM calls or compressed summaries. At retrieval time, SproutRAG uses hierarchical beam search to retrieve candidates at multiple granularities, capturing multi-sentence relevance beyond flat retrieval. The framework is trained end-to-end with a joint objective that improves both embeddings and tree structure. Experiments across four benchmarks spanning scientific, legal, and open-domain settings demonstrate that SproutRAG improves information efficiency (IE) by 6.1% on average over the strongest baseline. Code is available on https://github.com/AmirAbaskohi/SproutRAG.

</details>


### [89] [Want Better Synthetic Data? Steer It: Activation Steering for Low-Resource Language Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18389)
*Jan Cegin,Daniil Gurgurov,Yusser Al Ghussin,Simon Ostermann*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了激活控制（activation steering）在低资源语言合成数据生成中的应用，提出两种策略：语言控制（Language Steering）和质量控制（Quality Steering）。通过在多个开源大模型、不同层以及11种语言上进行实验，结果表明，早期层的激活控制能显著提升生成数据的多样性，并在下游任务中表现更优，尤其对低资源语言效果明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于少样本提示的合成数据生成方法成本高且易因词汇锚定导致多样性下降，亟需更高效、多样化的替代方案。

Method: 采用语言控制与质量控制两种激活控制策略，在零样本和少样本提示设置下，对多个大模型的不同层级进行实验，生成情感和主题分类数据并微调小型分类器进行评估。

Result: 早期层的激活控制显著提升了生成数据的多样性，并在多数情况下改善了下游任务性能，尤其对低资源语言更为有效。

Conclusion: 激活控制是一种高效且具有潜力的低资源语言合成数据生成方法，尤其在早期层应用时表现出色，可作为现有提示方法的有力补充。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have become an effective tool for synthetic data generation, including for low-resource languages, where generated data can improve downstream task performance. Current best-performing approaches typically rely on few-shot prompting with target-language examples, which increases inference costs and may reduce diversity through lexical anchoring. In this work, we investigate activation steering as an alternative for low-resource synthetic data generation. We study two steering strategies: Language Steering, which targets the linguistic identity of a language, and Quality Steering, which captures well-formedness by contrasting human-written and backtranslated text representations. We evaluate these methods across four open-source LLMs, multiple layers, and 11 typologically diverse languages by generating sentiment and topic classification data and finetuning smaller classifiers. Steering is applied in both zero-shot and few-shot prompting settings and compared against non-steered counterparts. Our results show that steering on early layers consistently improves the diversity of generated data while often yielding stronger downstream model performance, particularly for low-resource languages.

</details>


### [90] [JetFlow: Breaking the Scaling Ceiling of Speculative Decoding with Parallel Tree Drafting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18394)
*Lanxiang Hu,Zhaoxiang Feng,Yulun Wu,Haoran Yuan,Yujie Zhao,Yu-Yang Qian,Bojun Wang,Daxin Jiang,Yibo Zhu,Tajana Rosing,Hao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: JetFlow 是一种基于头的推测解码框架，结合了前向推理效率与分支级因果条件化，解决了以往方法在因果性与效率之间的权衡问题。它通过在冻结目标模型的融合隐藏状态上训练因果并行推测头，生成与目标模型自回归分解对齐的候选树，从而在更大推测预算下实现更长的接受前缀和更高的端到端加速。在数学、编码和聊天基准测试中，JetFlow 显著优于现有的双向头和树形推测解码基线，在H100 GPU上实现了高达9.64倍的加速（MATH-500）和4.58倍（开放对话任务），并通过vLLM集成展示了实际服务负载下的延迟优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推测解码方法受限于因果性与效率的权衡：自回归推测器虽具路径条件性但开销随树深增加；双向块扩散推测器虽高效但生成的分支无关边际常导致不一致树，浪费预算。需要一种兼具高效性和高接受率的新型推测解码机制。

Method: JetFlow 在冻结目标模型的融合隐藏状态上训练一个因果并行推测头，利用自回归因子化结构生成与目标模型一致的候选树，实现高效且一致的推测过程。该方法保持前向推理的低开销，同时引入分支级因果条件化以提升接受率。

Result: JetFlow 在多个基准（数学、编码、聊天）上均显著优于现有方法，最高实现9.64倍的推理加速（MATH-500），开放对话任务达4.58倍；在vLLM集成下进一步降低延迟，具备实际部署潜力。

Conclusion: JetFlow 通过创新的因果并行推测头设计，突破了传统推测解码的性能天花板，为大规模语言模型的高效推理提供了有效解决方案，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Speculative decoding (SD) accelerates autoregressive Large Language Models (LLMs) by drafting multiple tokens and verifying them in parallel, but it faces a scaling limitation: increasing the draft budget improves speed only when acceptance remains high and drafting overhead stays low. This ceiling has been difficult to break because prior head-based SD methods face a causality-efficiency dilemma. Autoregressive drafters produce path-conditioned candidates that are effective for tree speculative decoding with higher acceptance length, but their drafting cost grows with tree depth. Bidirectional block-diffusion drafters generate all positions in one pass, but their branch-agnostic marginals can form individually plausible yet mutually inconsistent trees, wasting budget and reducing acceptance. We propose JetFlow, a head-based SD framework that combines one-forward drafting efficiency with branch-wise causal conditioning. JetFlow trains a causal parallel draft head over fused hidden states from the frozen target model, producing candidate trees whose scores align with the target model's autoregressive factorization. This enables JetFlow to convert larger draft budgets into longer accepted prefixes and higher end-to-end speedup. Across math, coding, and chat benchmarks on dense and MoE Qwen3 models, JetFlow consistently outperforms bidirectional-head and tree-based SD baselines. On H100 GPUs, JetFlow achieves up to 9.64x speedup on MATH-500 and 4.58x on open-ended conversational workloads, with further latency gains demonstrated through vLLM integration under realistic serving loads. Our code and models are available at https://github.com/hao-ai-lab/JetFlow.

</details>


### [91] [CoreMem: Riemannian Retrieval and Fisher-Guided Distillation for Long-Term Memory in Dialogue Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18406)
*Jiaqi Chen,Yongqin Zeng,Shaoshen Chen,Yijian Zhang,Hai-Tao Zheng,Chunxia Ma,XiuTeng Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CoreMem 是一种基于信息几何的高效边缘-云记忆架构，旨在解决消费级硬件上长期对话代理的记忆瓶颈问题。它通过黎曼检索和费舍尔引导的离散标记压缩，实现了高维检索中的去中心化与语法结构保护，显著提升开放域和时间推理性能，并在8GB VRAM限制下实现高效运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统在资源受限设备上面临内存与计算瓶颈，且依赖启发式方法进行检索与压缩，缺乏统一理论基础，易出现中心化问题和语法碎片化。

Method: 提出Riemannian检索（使用局部自适应Fisher-Rao度量）和FDTD（基于费舍尔信息迹的层次化句到标记压缩），结合木尔比加速实现实时搜索，并通过信息几何建立压缩与KL散度之间的权衡。

Result: 在LOCOMO和LongMemEval-S基准上，核心指标分别提升4.51个百分点（开放域）和4.17个百分点（时间推理），并在8GB VRAM预算内稳定运行，验证了其在边缘设备上的可行性与优越性。

Conclusion: CoreMem通过信息几何统一框架，有效解决了边缘设备上长期记忆系统的效率与理论一致性难题，为构建可扩展、鲁棒的个性化对话代理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Personalized dialogue agents require continuous long-term memory to maintain coherent interactions across multiple sessions. However, deploying these capabilities on consumer-grade hardware (e.g., 8 GB VRAM edge devices) introduces severe memory and compute bottlenecks. Existing systems typically rely on isotropic cosine similarity for retrieval and heuristic rules for context compression. These approaches lack a unified theoretical foundation, frequently suffering from the hubness problem in high-dimensional retrieval and syntactic fragmentation during compression. To overcome these limitations, we propose CoreMem, a resource-efficient edge-cloud memory architecture fundamentally unified by information geometry. First, Riemannian retrieval replaces cosine matching with a locally adaptive Fisher-Rao metric, effectively penalizing hub memories via Mahalanobis distance with O(Ndr) Woodbury acceleration for real-time search. Second, Fisher-guided discrete token distillation (FDTD) introduces a hierarchical sentence-to-token compression mechanism. It derives sensitivity scores from Fisher information traces, providing a principled compression-KL tradeoff augmented with explicit structural syntax protection. Evaluated on the LOCOMO and LongMemEval-S benchmarks, CoreMem achieves strong accuracy improvements, yielding substantial gains in Open-domain (+4.51 pp) and Temporal (+4.17 pp) reasoning. Extensive profiling confirms that CoreMem operates seamlessly within a strict 8 GB VRAM budget, successfully bridging the gap between resource-constrained edge devices and the demand for theoretically grounded, lifelong memory agents.

### [92] [VISUALSKILL: Multimodal Skills for Computer-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18448)
*Ziyan Jiang,Li An,Yujian Liu,Jiabao Ji,Qiucheng Wu,Jacob Andreas,Yang Zhang,Shiyu Chang*

Main category: cs.CL

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 保留视觉图示而非将其转化为文字描述，显著提升了计算机使用代理对界面元素的识别能力和操作状态的验证能力，证明多模态技能在复杂、长周期任务中具有重要优势。

Abstract: Computer-use agents (CUAs) approach human-level performance on standardised benchmarks but still struggle on long-horizon tasks and unseen software. Existing skill libraries address this with reusable skills, but represent the skill artifact as text only, despite the visual nature of GUI interaction. We propose VISUALSKILL: a hierarchical multimodal skill, tailored to each target application and organised as a central index over per-topic files, which the agent consumes through a load_topic MCP tool that fetches the relevant topic's text and figures on demand. On two CUA benchmarks, CUA-World and OSExpert-Eval, a Claude Code CLI agent backed by Claude Opus 4.6 reaches an average score of 0.456 with VISUALSKILL, a +15.3 point absolute lift over the no-skill baseline (0.303). Against a matched text-only skill that is generated from the same source content and differs from VISUALSKILL only in modality, VISUALSKILL yields a further +8.3 point absolute gain over the matched text-only skill (0.373 vs. 0.456), providing direct evidence that retaining visual figures in the skill artifact, rather than verbalizing them away, helps the agent both identify UI elements and verify workflow state after each action. Our code is available at https://github.com/XMHZZ2018/VisualSkills.

Result: 提取出的数学相关参数存在部分跨语言重叠，最强重叠集中于中间层；英语产生最多的数学相关参数，而低资源语言的相关参数集较小。

We present a cross-lingual mechanistic analysis of mathematical reasoning in LLMs, enabling us to localize and compare model parameters that support mathematical reasoning across languages. We find that the extracted math-associated parameters exhibit partial cross-lingual overlap, with the strongest overlap concentrated in intermediate model layers. We further observe that English consistently produces the largest set of math-relevant parameters, whereas lower-resource languages reveal smaller sets of relevant parameters. These results suggest that math-related behavior in multilingual LLMs is neither fully language-invariant nor fully language-specific, but instead exhibits partial cross-lingual parameter overlap with systematic language-dependent differences.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for clinical text tasks such as summarization and revision. While most studies evaluate the fluency and coherence of LLM-generated text, whether LLMs correctly preserve diagnostic uncertainty remains underexplored. In clinical practice, phrases such as ``possible pneumonia'' communicate the strength of available evidence and directly guide decisions about follow-up testing and treatment. Altering these uncertainty expressions can change the clinical meaning entirely. In this paper, we systematically evaluated this problem in two steps.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Machine unlearning for large language models (LLMs) aims to remove specified knowledge while preserving the rest of the model's capabilities. However, the boundary between knowledge to forget and knowledge to retain is often unclear, since related and even distant information may be entangled in the model. In this paper, we study LLM unlearning from a data-centric perspective and measure how unlearning effects propagate from the forget set to same-domain and distant-domain knowledge. We find a consistent decay pattern: collateral damage is strongest near the forget set, weakens with semantic distance, but does not disappear at domain boundaries. We further ask whether such damage can be audited before unlearning is executed. We formulate forget-set auditing as a pre-unlearning prediction task and analyze which data features are most predictive of downstream damage. Our results show that interaction features between the forget set and evaluation set provide the strongest signals, suggesting that collateral damage is partly reflected in data geometry before model updates occur. These findings position forget-set auditing as an early warning tool for identifying risky unlearning runs and designing more reliable unlearning procedures.

### [98] [MCompassRAG: Topic Metadata as a Semantic Compass for Paragraph-Level Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18508)

TL;DR: MCompassRAG是一种基于元数据引导的检索框架，利用主题级信号作为语义导航，提升检索效率与精度。通过在嵌入空间中融合主题元数据并使用大模型教师蒸馏训练轻量检索器，在推理时实现无需额外大模型调用的主题感知检索，显著降低延迟并提升证据质量。在六个复杂检索基准上，平均信息效率提升8.24%，延迟低于最强基线模型的1/5。

Method: MCompassRAG通过在相同嵌入空间中丰富文档块的表示以包含主题元数据，并采用大语言模型教师蒸馏的方式训练一个轻量级检索器。在推理阶段，该框架基于主题感知机制进行检索，无需额外调用大模型，从而实现高效且高质量的检索。

Result: 在六个复杂检索基准测试中，MCompassRAG平均信息效率提升8.24%，同时延迟降低超过5倍，显著优于当前最先进的高效RAG基线模型。

Conclusion: MCompassRAG通过引入主题级元数据引导的检索机制，有效缓解了传统RAG系统在精度与效率之间的权衡问题，为复杂研究任务提供了更高效、更可靠的检索解决方案。代码已开源。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems depend critically on how documents are chunked and searched. Fine-grained chunks can improve retrieval precision but expand the search space, increasing latency and cost; larger chunks reduce the number of candidates but make dense similarity less reliable, as the representation for each chunk mixes multiple topics and introduces more semantic noise. This trade-off becomes especially limiting in deep research tasks, where retrieval must be both fast and precise across large, heterogeneous corpora. We introduce MCompassRAG, a metadata-guided retrieval framework that uses topic-level signals as a semantic compass for selecting relevant evidence. Instead of relying only on cosine similarity between queries and noisy chunk embeddings, MCompassRAG enriches chunk representations with topic metadata in the same embedding space and trains a lightweight retriever through LLM-teacher distillation. At inference time, MCompassRAG performs topic-aware retrieval without additional LLM calls, improving both efficiency and evidence quality. Across six complex retrieval benchmarks, MCompassRAG improves information efficiency (IE) by 8.24% on average with over 5 times lower latency than the strongest efficient RAG baselines. Code is available on https://github.com/AmirAbaskohi/MCompassRAG.

</details>

*Fan Xu,Jian Luo,MingWen Wang,GuoDong Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了基于语音的特征在中文方言细粒度区分中的有效性，提出了一种结合MFCC特征与端到端语音识别模型的混合方法，利用注意力机制提取方言相关词汇，并通过CNN融合词级嵌入与声学特征，在两个基准中文方言语料库上取得了优于现有方法的效果。

Method: 系统评估了基于语音的MFCC特征在CNN模型中的适用性；设计基于HMM-DNN的端到端语音识别模型以预测中文方言词汇；利用注意力机制提取与不同方言相关的判别性词汇；最后通过CNN融合词级嵌入与MFCC特征。

Result: 在两个基准中文方言语料库上的实验表明，所提出的语音驱动方法在细粒度中文方言区分任务中表现优异，显著优于当前最先进的方法。

Abstract: Language discrimination among similar languages, varieties, and dialects is a challenging natural language processing task. The traditional text-driven focus leads to poor results. In this paper, we explore the effectiveness of speech-driven features towards language discrimination among Chinese dialects. First, we systematically explore the appropriateness of speech-driven MFCC features towards CNN-based language discrimination. Then, we design an end-to-end speech recognition model based on HMM-DNN to predict Chinese dialect words. We adopt attention to extract the discriminative words related to different Chinese dialects. Finally, through a CNN, we combine the word-level embedding and the MFCC-based features. Evaluation of two benchmark Chinese dialect corpora shows the appropriateness and effectiveness of the proposed speech-driven approach to fine-grained Chinese dialect discrimination compared to the state-of-the-art methods.
